Loading theory "Draft.Templates" (required by "Draft.ExampleMoreTemplates" via "Draft.ExtrEqs")
datatype template_term
=
     t_empty
   | template_app of template_term * template_term
   | template_hole of int
   | template_var of int
datatype sign
= equals | greater_equals | greater_than | less_equals | less_than
datatype template
=
     template_bimplication of template * template
   | template_dunno
   | template_equation of template_term * template_term
   | template_implication of template list * template
   | template_inequation of sign * template_term * template_term
   | template_negation of template
   | template_predicate of template_term
constructor t_empty: template_term
constructor template_app: template_term * template_term -> template_term
constructor template_hole: int -> template_term
constructor template_var: int -> template_term
constructor equals: sign
constructor greater_equals: sign
constructor greater_than: sign
constructor less_equals: sign
constructor less_than: sign
constructor template_bimplication: template * template -> template
constructor template_dunno: template
constructor template_equation: template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_implication: template list * template -> template
constructor template_inequation:
   sign * template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_negation: template -> template
constructor template_predicate: template_term -> template

val indexOf = fn: ''a list -> ''a -> int -> int

   (indexname * typ) list -> (string * typ) list -> term -> template_term

val makeTemplatewithContext = fn: term -> term -> template
val lemma2template = fn: term -> template

val eqpattern =
   Pattern
    (
       Const ("HOL.Trueprop", "bool => prop") $
         (Const ("HOL.eq", "?'a => ?'a => bool") $
           Var (("_dummy_", 1), "?'a") $ Var (("_dummy_", 2), "?'a"))
       ):
   term Find_Theorems.criterion

   term Find_Theorems.criterion
val undefpattern =
   Pattern
    (
       Const ("HOL.Trueprop", "bool => prop") $
         (Const ("HOL.eq", "?'a => ?'a => bool") $
           Var (("_dummy_", 1), "?'a") $ Const ("HOL.undefined", "?'a"))
       ):
   term Find_Theorems.criterion

   term Find_Theorems.criterion

  fixes channel :: "nat => ('p * 'p) option"
    and trans :: "'p => 's => 's => bool"
    and send :: "nat => 'p => 'p => 's => 's => 'm => bool"
    and recv :: "nat => 'p => 'p => 's => 's => 'm => bool"

[| ALL p. (ps ?c p ~= None) = (ps ?d p ~= None); msgs ?c ?i = msgs ?d ?i;

   ~ regular_event ?ev |]

locale computation
  fixes channel :: "nat => ('a * 'a) option"
    and trans :: "'a => 'b => 'b => bool"
    and send :: "nat => 'a => 'a => 'b => 'b => 'c => bool"
    and recv :: "nat => 'a => 'a => 'b => 'b => 'c => bool"
    and init :: "('a, 'b, 'c) configuration"
    and final :: "('a, 'b, 'c) configuration"
  assumes "computation channel trans send recv init final"
[| states ?c ?p = states ?d ?p; ?c \<turnstile> ?ev \<mapsto> ?c';
   ?d \<turnstile> ?ev \<mapsto> ?d' |]
==> states ?d' ?p = states ?c' ?p
